 ) The Reserve Bank of India has issued guidelines to adopt a new 'token' system to further strengthen security in various card transactions, including debit and credit card transactions
 is token vyavastha kaa makasad bhugtan pranali kii suraksha ko majboot karnaa he
 This means replacing the actual details of the card with a specific alternative code token, the code itself will be a unique arrangement
 point of cell (pioes) terminlon, quick respance (kuar) code bhugtan ke liye vaastavik card byore ke sthaan par card se samparkrhit tareeke se lenden ke liye is token kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 The central bank said that the facility of transaction with token card will be available through mobile phones and tablets at present, it will be expanded later to other devices based on the experience gained
 rigerv bank kii vijyapti main kaha gaya he ki card ke tokanikaran or token vyavastha se hataane kaa kaam keval adhikrut card network dwaara hi kiya jayega, isamen mul praathmik khaataa number (pieen) kii recovery bhi praadhikrut card network se hi ho sakegi
 The customer will not have to pay any fee for availing this service
 rigerv bank ne kaha he ki card ke liye token sevaayen shuru karne se pehle praadhikrut card bhugtan network ko pranali kii ek nishchit avadhi main lekhapariksha ke liye pranali sthapit kerani hogi

 Every year millions of people die in India waiting for organ donation
 bharat main abhi bhi organ donneton ko lekar logon main jaagrukta nahin he
 Due to this, the death toll is many times more than other countries
 isi kadi main logon ko jaagruk karne ke liye medanta aspataal or mohan foundation ne saath mil kar ek pradarshnee kaa aayojan kiya he
